**纺工与牧师**

> [[Liston Pope]]

---
# Preface
**序**

NEARLY everybody has notions about the proper role of the church in economic affairs. Businessmen and labor leaders, laymen and ministers disagree emphatically, and frequently accuse each other of apostasy. On the one hand, the church is admonished to confine its attention to the spiritual needs of its parishioners lest its inclusive fellowship be broken or its gospel compromised. On the other, ministers are summoned to fearless proclamation of the Kingdom of God in social terms, with less retreat into surplices and cloisters and more attention to practices of factory and market place. The church is blamed for its indifference and praised for minding its own business, commended as an agent of social salvation and denounced as a haven for meddling, acclaimed as a guarantor of social stability and cursed as an insidious peddler of dope.

> 几乎每个人对于教会在经济事务中应扮演的角色都有自己的见解。商界领袖与工会代表、普通信徒与神职人员之间常存在尖锐分歧，并时常相互指责对方背弃信仰。一方面，有人告诫教会应仅关注信徒的精神需求，以免其包容性的团契关系破裂或福音信息遭到妥协。另一方面，人们呼吁神职人员勇敢地以社会性语言宣告上帝的国度，减少对圣职服饰与修道院的依赖，更多地关注工厂与市场的实际运作。教会既因冷漠态度受到指责，又因恪守本职获得赞许；既被誉为社会救赎的媒介，又被斥为多管闲事的避风港；既被推崇为社会稳定的保障者，又被诅咒为暗中传播麻醉剂的贩子。

Despite the controversy, which is of long standing, very little study of the actual role of the church in economic society has been undertaken. Social philosophers have advanced various hypotheses, among which the theories of Marx and Max Weber are best known. Historians have treated the question occasionally, and have been especially interested in the rough coincidence of the rise of Protestantism and capitalism. Social scientists have described painstakingly the functions of religion in preliterate economies, but have devoted a surprisingly small amount of attention to contemporary modes of the problem. No coherent, refined body of knowledge about the function of the church in Western economic systems is available and argument proceeds without benefit of adequate data.

> 尽管这一争议由来已久，但关于教会在经济社会中实际角色的研究却寥寥无几。社会哲学家们提出了多种假说，其中以 Marx 与 Max Weber 的理论最为著名。历史学者偶尔会探讨这一问题，并对新教兴起与资本主义发展之间的大致同步性表现出特别兴趣。社会科学家们曾细致描述宗教在前文字社会中的经济功能，却对当代社会中的相关问题模式关注甚少。目前尚缺乏关于教会在西方经济体系中功能的系统而精确的知识体系，相关讨论往往在没有充足数据支撑的情况下进行。

The multiplicity of popular notions and sociological theories can be reduced to six types of possible relation between religious and economic institutions. Religious institutions, in relation to economic institutions, might be:

*in dynamic terms,*
- a source of economic changes
- a product of prior economic changes

*in static terms,*
- a sanction on the prevailing economic organization and economic culture
- an antagonist to the prevailing economic organization and economic culture

*in purposive-functional terms,*
- indifferent to the economic sphere as such
- irrelevant to economic results, in the sense that no effective contact is established with economic realities.

> 关于宗教与经济制度之间可能存在的多重流行观念和社会学理论，可以归纳为六种基本关系类型。  
> 
> *从动态角度来看，宗教制度可能：*  
> - 成为经济变革的源头  
> - 作为先前经济变革的产物  
> 
> *从静态角度来看，宗教制度可能：*  
> - 对主流经济组织与经济文化起到认可与巩固作用  
> - 对主流经济组织与经济文化形成对抗与挑战  
> 
> *从目的与功能角度来看，宗教制度可能：*  
> - 对经济领域本身持中立态度  
> - 与经济结果无关，即未能与经济活动现实建立有效联系

Gaston County, North Carolina, affords an advantageous social context in which to test at first hand the relative importance of these diverse modes of relationship. Within the memory of its oldest inhabitants, an agricultural economy has been superseded by phenomenal industrial development. As in England and New England decades earlier, the textile industry has been a harbinger of industrial revolution, and many of the economic and social patterns attending its previous cycles have been recapitulated at accelerated speed. Two decad Piedmont area from Danville to Birmingham, and Gaston County, lying nearly at the geographical cees after the Civil War, cotton mills began to appear in unprecedented number throughout the Southernnter of the area, became a center and symbol of industrial transformation. A survey in 1927 revealed that Gastonia, the principal town in the county, had come to have more looms and spindles within a radius of 100 miles than any other Southern city, with a total of 570 textile plants and nearly 10 million spindles in this range of proximity. Though it had been devoted almost exclusively to agricultural pursuits in 1880, the county was able in 1939 to claim a larger number of textile plants than any other county in the world, and was manufacturing 80 per cent of the fine combed cotton yarn produced in the United States. Only seventeen by twenty miles in extent, its landscape teems now with cotton mills and industrial villages. Here, then, is a compact, manageable situation in which economic institutions have undergone drastic change recently enough to allow direct observation of the part played by religious institutions in the process.

> North Carolina 的 Gaston County 提供了一个有利的社会环境，使我们能够直接检验这些不同关系模式的相对重要性。在该县最年长居民的记忆中，农业经济已被迅猛的工业发展所取代。正如几十年前的 England 和 New England 一样，纺织业一直是工业革命的先驱，其先前周期所伴随的许多经济与社会模式也以更快的速度在此地重现。内战结束 20 年后，棉纺厂开始以前所未有的数量出现在从 Danville 到 Birmingham 的 Southern Piedmont 地区，而 Gaston County 几乎位于该地区的地理中心，成为工业转型的中心和象征。1927 年的一项调查显示，Gastonia 作为该县的主要城镇，在 100 英里半径内拥有比任何其他南方城市更多的织机和纺锤，在这个接近范围内总共有 570 家纺织厂和近 1000 万纺锤。尽管在 1880 年几乎完全致力于农业，该县在 1939 年能够声称拥有比世界上任何其他县更多的纺织厂，并且制造了美国生产的精细梳棉纱的 80%。该县地域仅 17 乘 20 英里，如今却遍布棉纺厂与工业村落。因此，这里形成了一种紧凑而易于研究的局面：经济制度在近期经历了剧烈变革，使得我们能够直接观察宗教制度在此过程中所扮演的角色。

As compared with other counties in which comparable transformations have occurred, Gaston County offers several distinct advantages to the student of social patterns. It is not necessarily "typical" or "average"—whatever those terms may mean—of other counties in the vicinity or the nation. Things have happened in Gaston County, such as a violent Communist challenge to its economic organization, which are fairly unique, but by the same token are highly illuminating for other regions where deep-laid social textures have not been similarly laid open for examination. In respect to economic institutions the county is more developed and less diversified than many others. Its religious institutions, on the other hand, are more highly diversified; Presbyterian and Lutheran settlers have been outnumbered by Methodist and Baptist newcomers and there is a generous representation of other Protestants and of Roman Catholics. In the simplicity of its economic forms and the diversity of its religious forms, the county provides a significant and governable context in which to observe interrelations of the two spheres.

> 与其他发生过类似转型的县相比，Gaston County 为研究社会模式的学生提供了若干独特的优势。它未必是周边或全国其他县的“典型”或“平均”代表——无论这些术语意味着什么。加斯顿县曾发生过一些相当独特的事情，例如对当地经济组织的暴力共产主义挑战，但正因如此，这些事件为其他社会深层结构尚未被如此公开检视的地区提供了极具启发性的参照。在经济制度方面，该县比许多其他地区更为发达且结构相对单一。而其宗教制度则呈现出更高程度的多样性：原先的长老会和路德宗教徒已被卫理宗与浸信会信徒超越，其他新教派别和罗马天主教也有广泛代表。凭借其经济形态的单一性与宗教形态的多样性，该县为观察这两个领域之间的相互关系提供了重要且可控的研究背景。

The interaction of churches and cotton mills in Gaston County since 1880 has proceeded in three modes of institutional life. First of all, there have been reciprocal relations in growth, i.e., expansion, quantitative increase in salient respects, qualitative differentiation and proliferation within each type of institution as compared with the other. Secondly, restraining and regulatory procedures have been worked out between the two types of institution, illustrative of the perennial problem of social integration and control. Last of all, the mills and churches have gone through a severe crisis together, and in so doing revealed fundamental relationships to each other which are normally obscured. A fourth conceivable mode, institutional deterioration, is not yet clearly observable in this particular county.

> 自 1880 年以来，Gaston County 的教堂与棉纺厂之间的互动呈现出三种制度生活模式。首先，两者在增长方面存在相互促进的关系，即扩张、显著方面的数量增长、以及相较于另一种制度，各自内部发生的质量分化和多样化。其次，两种制度之间形成了制约与调节的机制，这体现了社会整合与控制这一长期存在的问题。最后，棉纺厂与教堂共同经历了一场严峻的危机，并在此过程中揭示了通常被掩盖的彼此间根本性关联。至于第四种可能存在的模式——制度衰退，在该具体县区尚未明显显现。

In the pages that follow, the focus of interest lies in institutions rather than in individuals or in such imponderables as "religion" or "economic welfare." Particular, observable cotton mills and churches are the characters in the story to be unfolded. Most often they speak through their chief executives, the mill managers and ministers, but these spokesmen are hedged about at every turn by the traditions and necessities of the institutions they represent. Occasionally it is of value to speculate on the hidden purposes and motives of these executives; though such procedure is always hazardous, it is sometimes necessary for interpretation of the lines that are spoken. Individuals are represented as significant, however, only insofar as they represent institutions.\

> 在接下来的页面中，兴趣焦点在于制度，而非个人或诸如“宗教”或“经济福利”这类难以估量的事物。具体、可观察的棉纺厂和教堂是即将展开的故事中的角色。大多数时候，它们通过其首席执行官——即工厂经理和牧师——发言，但这些发言人处处受到他们所代表制度的传统和必要性的制约。偶尔，推测这些执行者的隐藏目的和动机是有价值的；尽管这种做法总是危险的，但有时对于解读他们所说的话是必要的。然而，个人只有在代表制度时才被描绘为重要。

The cast of characters is limited in other respects. Two institutions carry on a dialogue, rather than conduct a forum in which all aspects of community life may be represented. In more technical parlance, analysis in this volume is vertical rather than horizontal in scope; it probes into the roles of two institutions over a period of sixty years and explores the relations between them, rather than undertakes exposition of all social phenomena in the locale. Politics, leisure activities, family relations, education—these and many other fellow townsmen beckon frequently to the main characters, and occasionally it is necessary to pause for a brief word with them, but hurriedly, lest the thread of the ongoing conversation be lost.

> 人物角色在其他方面也受到限制。本研究中仅有两家机构持续进行对话，而非举办一个能代表社区生活方方面面的论坛。用更专业的术语来说，本书的分析在范围上是垂直而非水平的；它深入探究了两家机构在六十年间的角色演变，并剖析二者之间的关系，而非对当地所有社会现象进行全景式阐述。政治、休闲活动、家庭关系、教育——这些以及其他众多同镇居民时常向主要角色招手示意，偶尔需要驻足与他们简短交流，但总是匆匆而过，唯恐打断持续对话的主线。

Even the most interesting characters of all, the Negro population and Negro churches, must be largely excluded. They are not directly relevant to the immediate problem involved, and adequate interpretation of them presents methodological difficulties well-nigh insuperable. Of 12,392 Negroes in the county in 1930, less than 400 were employed in cotton mills, and even these were marginal workers. Nor does the presence of a Negro population, lacking direct participation in the economic or religious life of the larger community, constitute in any significant sense a control group, because the race line cuts across all other factors. Furthermore, methods of research entirely different from those entailed for white churches are necessary for colored churches; it is virtually impossible to secure information about the latter for the years prior to 1920 because written records are scarce and memories are extremely fallible and contradictory. Almost without exception, therefore, generalizations and statistics in subsequent pages do not include the Negro, though attempts to clarify his status are introduced occasionally.

> 即便在所有群体中最具特色的黑人人口与黑人教会，也必须被大幅排除在讨论之外。他们与当前涉及的核心问题并无直接关联，且对其进行充分阐释所面临的方法论难题几乎无法克服。1930 年该县共有 12,392 名黑人，其中受雇于棉纺厂者不足 400 人，且这些工人均处于边缘岗位。黑人群体因未广泛参与更大型社区的经济或宗教生活，其存在亦无法在显著意义上构成对照组——种族界限横贯所有其他因素。此外，研究黑人教会所需的方法与白人教会截然不同；要获取 1920 年前黑人教会的相关信息几乎不可能，因为书面记录稀缺，而记忆又极不可靠且矛盾重重。因此，除偶尔尝试阐明其状况外，后文中的概括与统计数据几乎无一例外地将黑人群体排除在外。

A combination of observational and historical methods has been used in gathering material. For several months in 1938 and 1939 the author lived in Gaston County, making detailed studies and having interviews with hundreds of residents of all types. Field work ended on the day the second World War began, but two subsequent visits have not revealed any significant changes in pattern. Pertinent literary sources were discovered through research in more than a dozen libraries in various parts of the country and through the examination of manuscripts, letters, clippings, and pamphlets collected by several individuals. About forty unpublished manuscripts and approximately twenty theses written by graduate students have been especially helpful. Compilation of statistics for each decennial year from 1880 to the present involved research in the minutes of ecclesiastical bodies, in textile journals, and in the respective Federal censuses, including those reports of the 1940 Census which are available to date.

> 观察法和历史法的结合被用于收集材料。在 1938 年和 1939 年的几个月里，作者住在 Gaston County，进行详细研究并采访了数百名各类居民。实地工作结束于第二次世界大战开始的那一天，但随后的两次访问并未揭示任何显著的模式变化。相关的文献来源通过在全国各地十几个图书馆的研究以及通过检查由几位个人收集的手稿、信件、剪报和小册子而被发现。大约四十份未发表的手稿和大约二十篇由研究生撰写的论文特别有帮助。为从 1880 年至今的每个十年期编制统计数据涉及对教会机构会议记录、纺织期刊以及各自联邦人口普查的研究，包括截至目前的 1940 年人口普查报告。

In a somewhat different and more extensive form, the material on which this volume is based was presented as a dissertation in partial fulfillment of the requirements for the degree of Doctor of Philosophy at Yale University, and in that connection was awarded the John Addison Porter Prize for the year 1940. A copy of the original manuscript, containing a number of tables, graphs, documentary proofs, and similar paraphernalia which have been omitted from the published volume, is on file in the Sterling Memorial Library of Yale University and is available to anyone having legitimate need of it.

> 在某种程度上经过调整与扩充后，本书所依据的材料曾作为耶鲁大学哲学博士学位要求的部分成果以论文形式提交，并因此荣获 1940 年度的 John Addison Porter 奖。原稿副本存于耶鲁大学 Sterling Memorial 图书馆，其中包含大量图表、文献证据及类似辅助材料，这些内容在出版版本中已被省略，可供有正当需要的人士查阅使用。

Gratitude for assistance is due to more persons than it is possible to mention. Innumerable residents of Gaston County have provided valuable help, but their names, except where public property, must be omitted here and throughout this volume for reasons which they will doubtless appreciate. This necessity has weakened the direct validation of many assertions and conclusions, but seems inescapable. Professors E. Wight Bakke, Charles A. Ellwood, James Leyburn, Broadus Mitchell, H. Richard Niebuhr, and Howard W. Odum have contributed immeasurably to background, criticism, and encouragement, directly and indirectly. Sources and files of information which would have been lost, except for their diligence, were made available by Dr. James Myers, Dr. James Dombrowski, Miss Harriet Herring, Mr. Ewing C. Baskette, and Mr. Willis Weatherford. Special help in library research was given by the late Dr. S. M. Tenney of the Montreat Historical Foundation, Dr. G. W. Paschal of Wake Forest College, Miss Charlotte Blake of the Gastonia Public Library, Miss Janet Welton of the Presbyterian Committee on Publication in Richmond, and officials of the Ruthenberg Library in New York. Editors Douglas G. Woolf and William B. Dall of the Textile World opened a rare file of statistics on the textile industry, and Mrs. Mildred Gwin Barnwell, executive secretary of the Southern Combed Yarn Spinners Association, helped to interpret more recent developments in the industry. Mr. Henry I. Adams and Miss Lucy Randolph Mason of the Textile Workers Union of America gave insight into the peculiar problems of the labor movement in mill villages. Former Governor Clyde R. Hoey of North Carolina and strike leader Fred E. Beal told of their respective roles in the Gastonia strike of 1929 and were equally gracious, the one in his office in the state capitol, the other in a state prison. To each and all of these persons sincere gratitude is extended. None of them is to be held responsible for the interpretations and conclusions presented here; many of them would doubtless disagree heartily at various points.

> 感激之情应归于众多无法一一提及的人。Gaston County 的无数居民提供了宝贵的帮助，但他们的名字，除非是公共财产，必须在这里和整卷中省略，原因他们无疑会理解。这种必要性削弱了许多断言和结论的直接验证，但似乎是不可避免的。教授们如 E. Wight Bakke、Charles A. Ellwood、James Leyburn、Broadus Mitchell、H. Richard Niebuhr 和 Howard W. Odum 在背景、批评和鼓励方面做出了不可估量的贡献，无论是直接还是间接。信息的来源和文件，若非他们的勤奋，本已丢失，现由 Dr. James Myers、Dr. James Dombrowski、Miss Harriet Herring、Mr. Ewing C. Baskette 和 Mr. Willis Weatherford 提供。图书馆研究的特殊帮助由 Montreat Historical Foundation 的已故 Dr. S. M. Tenney、Wake Forest College 的 Dr. G. W. Paschal、Gastonia Public Library 的 Miss Charlotte Blake、Richmond 的 Presbyterian Committee on Publication 的 Miss Janet Welton 以及 New York 的 Ruthenberg Library 的官员提供。Textile World 的编辑 Douglas G. Woolf 和 William B. Dall 开放了关于纺织工业的稀有统计文件，而 Southern Combed Yarn Spinners Association 的执行秘书 Mrs. Mildred Gwin Barnwell 帮助解释了该行业更近的发展。Textile Workers Union of America 的 Mr. Henry I. Adams 和 Miss Lucy Randolph Mason 提供了对工厂村庄中劳工运动特殊问题的见解。North Carolina 的前州长 Clyde R. Hoey 和罢工领袖 Fred E. Beal 讲述了他们在 1929 年 Gastonia 罢工中的各自角色，并且同样亲切，一个在州首府的办公室，另一个在州监狱。向每一位和所有这些人士致以诚挚的感激。他们中没有人应对这里提出的解释和结论负责；他们中的许多人无疑会在各种点上热烈地不同意。

For reading the manuscript and making useful suggestions, especial thanks are due to Dean Luther A. Weigle, Miss Harriet Herring, Dr. James Myers, Professor Raymond Morris, and Mr. Jonathan Daniels. Dean Weigle and several officials of the Yale University Press have been considerate and helpful in bringing the material to publication. Mr. Claude Whitehead gave able assistance in compilation of statistics. Mrs. Esther Davison manifested extraordinary patience, skill, and perseverance in transcribing a difficult manuscript into legibility. My parents in North Carolina have greatly facilitated the process of research, and my wife has helped in innumerable ways with patience and enthusiasm.

> 对于阅读手稿并提出有益建议方面，特别感谢 Dean Luther A. Weigle、Miss Harriet Herring、Dr. James Myers、Professor Raymond Morris 和 Mr. Jonathan Daniels。Dean Weigle 和 Yale University Press 的几位官员，在将材料出版方面表现得体贴和有帮助。Mr. Claude Whitehead 在统计数据的汇编中提供了能干的协助。Mrs. Esther Davison 在将一份难以辨认的手稿转录成清晰可读的过程中，展现了非凡的耐心、技能和毅力。我在 North Carolina 的父母极大地促进了研究过程，而我的妻子以耐心和热情在无数方面提供了帮助。

<div style=text-align:right>L.P.</div>

*New Haven, Connecticut,*
	*December 5, 1941.*

> 利·波
> 
> *于美国康涅狄格州纽黑文，*
> 
> *1941年12月5日。*

---
# INTRODUCTION

> RICHARD A. PETERSON and N. J. DEMERATH Ⅲ

LISTON POPE's Millhands and Preachers is by now a classic, and yet the term "classic" is confusing in itself. It often refers to age and not agelessness. It sometimes signifies a work that is more important for its errors than its accuracies. Such is not our usage. A genuine classic confronts central theoretical issues, has continued relevance to persisting substantive problems, contributes important data, and serves as a model for research in any era. Millhands and Preachers qualifies on all counts, and this new publication of it is as much a guide to the future as a landmark of the past.

> [[Liston Pope|利斯顿·波普]] 的《Millhands and Preachers》如今已成为一部经典之作，然而“经典”这一术语本身却常令人困惑。它往往指向的是年代久远，而非永恒不朽。有时，它意味着那些因其错误比其准确之处更具重要性而著称的作品。但这并非我们在此的用法。一部真正的经典直面核心理论议题，对持续存在的实质性问题具有长久的关联性，贡献重要数据，并在任何时代都能作为研究范本。《Millhands and Preachers》在所有这些方面均符合标准，而此次新版的面世，既是对过去的一座里程碑，亦是对未来的一份指引。

In this book Liston Pope describes the historical background and surrounding events of a strike which occurred in a single cotton mill in the small city of Gastonia, North Carolina, in 1929. No strike has received more penetrating analysis, [^0-1-1]  and seldom has one particular episode been made to illumine so many others. Pope is among the rare men who are able to depict the particular so as to elucidate the general. The forces Gastonia witnessed in 1929 emerge time and again among the crucial influences in social history. The strike did little for the cause of labor, but this study of it has made a great contribution to the social sciences.

> 在本书中，Liston Pope 描述了 1929 年发生于北卡罗来纳州小城 Gastonia 一家棉纺厂的罢工所处的历史背景及相关事件。没有任何一次罢工曾受到如此深入的剖析，[^0-1-1]也很少有某个孤立事件能如此深刻地揭示如此众多的其他事件。Pope 是少数几位能够通过描绘具体事例来阐明普遍规律的人物之一。1929 年 Gastonia 所见证的种种力量，在社会历史的关键影响因素中反复显现。此次罢工本身对劳工运动贡献甚微，但对它的研究却为社会科学做出了巨大贡献。

Pope's overriding concern is with the role of the church in social affairs and its frequent vassalage to economic leaders.

> Pope 最关切的是教会参与社会事务的角色，以及它常常屈从于经济领袖的现象。

In exploring the topic, he contributes insights to many related issues, including the distinction between church and sect, the relation between social class and religion, the impact of economic development and technological change on the community, the conflict between local and societal interests, the struggle for industrial peace through industrial democracy, and the causes and consequences of mob behavior. Then, too, Millhands and Preachers carries implicit messages for a host of other research interests. For example, a great deal of the tension between management and labor runs parallel to the current friction between Negroes and whites. The ways in which Southern communities have reacted to civil rights workers are reminiscent of Gastonia's reaction to outside union organizers.

> 在探讨这一主题时，他为许多相关问题提供了见解，包括教会与教派的区分、社会阶层与宗教的关系、经济发展与技术变革对社区的影响、地方利益与社会利益之间的冲突、通过工业民主争取产业和平的斗争，以及群体行为的成因与后果。此外，《Millhands and Preachers》还隐含着对其他诸多研究领域的启示。例如，管理层与劳工之间的紧张关系，在很大程度上与当前黑人与白人之间的摩擦存在相似之处。南方社区对民权工作者的反应方式，令人联想到 Gastonia 当年对外来工会组织者的态度。

But while the volume is important for students of religion, industrial sociology, stratification, social disorganization, and race relations, its manifold relevance is not all that recommends it. Its style is equally appealing. The commentary is lucid and compelling. Points are made through graphic illustrations, often in the words of the actors themselves. How many studies can offer a running summary through quotations like the following?

> 然而，尽管本书的体量对研究宗教、工业社会学、阶层分化、社会解构及种族关系的学者具有重要意义，其多重关联性并非唯一的推荐理由。其行文风格同样引人入胜。论述清晰透彻且富有说服力。观点常通过生动的例证呈现，其中不乏当事人亲述的鲜活话语。有多少研究能像本书这样，通过如下引文持续勾勒出完整的叙事脉络？
 
- [From an industrial pioneer] “We make American citizens, and run cotton mills to pay the expenses.”[^0-1-2]

- [From a Gastonia mill official] “Belonging to a church, and attending it, makes a man a better worker. It makes him more complacent—no, that’s not the word. It makes him more resigned—that's not the word either, but you get the general idea.” [And indeed Pope did.]  [^0-1-3]

- Singing "Praise God from Whom All Blessings Flow," the mob rushed into a boardinghouse in Gastonia, seized three N.T.W.U. organizers, and carried them into an adjoining county, where they were beaten and abandoned.[^0-1-4]

> - [一位工业先驱说]：“我们培养美国公民，而经营棉纺厂只是为了支付费用。”
> 
> - [一位 Gastonia 纺织厂官员说]：“加入教会并去参加礼拜，能让一个人成为更好的工人。这让他更顺从——不，这不是我要用的词。这让他更安于现状——这个词也不对，但你能明白我的意思。”[而 Pope 确实明白了。]
> 
> - 一群暴徒一边高唱“赞美上帝，万福之源”，一边冲进 Gastonia 的一家寄宿公寓，抓走了三名 N.T.W.U.（全国纺织工人联合会）组织者，并将他们带到邻县，毒打后弃之不顾。

Throughout the work, Pope honors the admonition to "stay close to the data." He avoids theoretical abstractions that depart from the stuff of Gaston County life. In letting the data speak for themselves, he is reluctant to speak beyond them. This lends a beguiling air of verisimilitude to the analysis. But the strategy has its costs as well as its rewards. Precisely because Pope shies clear of generalization himself, the reader is left a free hand to generalize on his own.<sup>5</sup> Clearly, however, such generalization requires limits and perspective.

> 在整部作品中，Pope 始终遵循着“紧贴数据”的劝诫。他避免脱离加斯顿县生活本质的理论抽象。通过让数据自己说话，他不愿做出超越数据本身的解读。这为分析赋予了一种诱人的真实感。但此种策略既带来收益，亦需付出代价。正因 Pope 本人刻意回避概括性结论，读者便被赋予了自由发挥、自行概括的空间。[^0-1-5] 然而显然，这种概括必须受到一定的界限与视角的约束。

Such a perspective is the goal of the present introduction. Written by two sociologists with a common interest in the community and respective specialties in the realms of industry and religion, this contribution is more theoretical than theological. First, we will seek historical perspective by indicating that the situation in Gastonia in 1929 was in many ways closer to the situation in eighteenth- and nineteenth-century Europe than it is to the larger American community of the 1960's. We will examine some of the broader variables that affect the innovation and influence of the church in secular affairs and suggest that the churches need not always be the "prisoner" they seemed to be in Gastonia. We will also note some of the peculiarities of the textile industry, peculiarities that trace back into nineteenth-century England and that might alone account for the abortiveness of the Gastonia strike. Finally, we will try to draw out the implications of Pope's analysis for the racial agony in the South. This is not meant, however, to exhaust the important facets of the book. Indeed, we might challenge any reader to finish the book without arriving at a new insight or a new formulation for a problem that concerns him, but which we omit. It is this stimulation that gives the work a unique freshness to couple with its enduring scholarship. It is this same stimulation that has produced an introduction that goes beyond the conventional panegyric.

> 这样的视角是本次引言的目标。由两位对社区有共同兴趣、分别在工业和宗教领域有专长的社会学家撰写，这篇贡献更偏向理论而非神学。首先，我们将通过指出 1929 年 Gastonia 的情况在许多方面更接近 18 世纪和 19 世纪的欧洲，而不是 1960 年代的美国大社区，来寻求历史视角。我们将审视一些影响教会在世俗事务中创新和影响力的更广泛变量，并建议教会不必总是像在 Gastonia 那样成为“囚徒”。我们还将注意到纺织业的一些特性，这些特性可以追溯到 19 世纪的 England，并且可能单独解释 Gastonia 罢工的失败。最后，我们将尝试引出 Pope 的分析对南方种族痛苦的启示。然而，这并非意在穷尽本书的重要方面。事实上，我们可能会挑战任何读者在读完本书后，不会对某个他关心但我们未提及的问题获得新的见解或新的表述。正是这种刺激赋予了这部作品独特的清新感，与其持久的学术性相结合。正是同样的刺激产生了一篇超越传统颂词的引言。

---

[^0-1-1]: Additional empirical studies of strikes, analyzed from various perspectives, include: E. T. Hiller, The Strike (Chicago, University of Chicago Press, 1928); Richard T. LaPiere, "The General Strike in San Francisco: A Study of the Revolutionary Pattern," Sociology and Social Research, 19 (March-April, 1935), 355-363; Ruth McKenny, Industrial Valley (New York, Harcourt-Brace & Co., 1939); Almond Lindsey, The Pullman Strike (Chicago, University of Chicago Press, 1942); W. Lloyd Warner and J. O. Low, The Social System of the Modern Factory; The Strike: A Social Analysis (New Haven, Yale University Press, 1947); J. F. Scott and G. C. Homans, "Reflections on the Wildcat Strike," American Sociological Review, 12 (June, 1947), 278-287; K. G. J. C. Knowles, *Strikes: A Study in Industrial Conflict* (Oxford, Blackwell, 1952); Alvin W. Gouldner, *Wildcat Strike* (Yellow Springs, Antioch Press, 1954); Bernard Karsh, *Diary of a Strike* (Urbana, University of Illinois Press, 1958).
```
从不同角度分析的罢工的额外实证研究包括：E. T. Hiller, The Strike (Chicago, University of Chicago Press, 1928); Richard T. LaPiere, "The General Strike in San Francisco: A Study of the Revolutionary Pattern," Sociology and Social Research, 19 (March-April, 1935), 355-363; Ruth McKenny, Industrial Valley (New York, Harcourt-Brace & Co., 1939); Almond Lindsey, The Pullman Strike (Chicago, University of Chicago Press, 1942); W. Lloyd Warner and J. O. Low, The Social System of the Modern Factory; The Strike: A Social Analysis (New Haven, Yale University Press, 1947); J. F. Scott and G. C. Homans, "Reflections on the Wildcat Strike," American Sociological Review, 12 (June, 1947), 278-287; K. G. J. C. Knowles, Strikes: A Study in Industrial Conflict (Oxford, Blackwell, 1952); Alvin W. Gouldner, Wildcat Strike (Yellow Springs, Antioch Press, 1954); Bernard Karsh, Diary of a Strike (Urbana, University of Illinois Press, 1958).
```

[^0-1-2]: Millhands and Preachers, p. 16 (1942 edition).

[^0-1-3]: Ibid., p. 31.

[^0-1-4]: Ibid., pp. 291-292.

[^0-1-5]: Here Pope is similar to Max Weber. Both men have suffered interpretive injustice at the hands of those anxious to transform case studies into systematic theories. For example, in The Protestant Ethic and the Spirit of Capitalism (New York, Charles Scribner's Sons, 1958), Weber is often accused of arguing not only that Protestantism "caused" the rise of capitalism but also that religious change precedes economic change generally. In fact, Weber went to great pains to avoid both misconceptions. He was suspicious of unilateral causal interpretations of whatever sort. His conclusions were models of restraint. As a gauge of the further similarity between Pope and Weber in these respects, note the Weberian rhetoric in the following statement from Millhands and Preachers: "Support given by the churches was of genuine service in crystallizing and extending the new interest in industry. If religious sanction was in part a product of prior economic developments, it was a simultaneous product and a source of further developments along the same line. Certainly it was only one factor in bringing the mills to birth, but few contributions to the growth of industry were of greater importance than the early approval tendered by the churches" (p. 27, 1942 edition). Nonetheless, Pope perceived the importance of the churches in quite a different way from Weber. As we shall suggest later, Pope emphasizes the churches' role in insuring a docile labor force, whereas Weber stresses theology's role in assuaging and stimulating the capitalists themselves.
`此处 Pope 与 Max Weber 颇为相似。两人都曾遭受解释性不公，被那些急于将个案研究转化为系统理论的人所误读。例如在《新教伦理与资本主义精神》（纽约，Charles Scribner's Sons 出版社，1958 年）中，Weber 常被指责不仅主张新教“导致”了资本主义的兴起，还认为宗教变革通常先于经济变革。事实上，Weber 竭力避免这两种误解。他对任何形式的单向因果解释都持怀疑态度，其结论堪称克制典范。若要进一步衡量 Pope 与 Weber 在这些方面的相似性，可注意《Millhands and Preachers》中这段颇具韦伯式修辞的论述："教会提供的支持确实有助于凝聚并扩展对工业的新兴兴趣。如果说宗教认可部分源自先前的经济发展，那么它既是同步产物，也是推动同方向进一步发展的源泉。诚然，这仅是催生工厂的诸多因素之一，但对工业增长而言，很少有比教会早期给予的认可更重要的贡献了"（1942 年版第 27 页）。然而，Pope 对教会重要性的理解方式与 Weber 截然不同。正如后文将指出的，Pope 强调教会在确保驯顺劳动力方面的作用，而 Weber 则着重于神学在安抚与激励资本家群体方面扮演的角色。`

## Religion and the Economy in Gastonia: Historical Accident or Commonplace?
**加斯顿尼亚的宗教与经济：历史偶然还是普遍现象？**

Certainly the most striking of Pope's findings is the extent to which the millhands were deserted by the preachers. The churches were inextricably bound to mill management by their finances if not by their ideology. Organized religion was a key instrument in creating a manipulable labor force and in resisting the union's effort to break with the exploitative status quo. Ministers not only justified management practices; they were mute in reaction to the violent recriminations exerted by the community against the union organizers. But if this was the case in the Gastonia of 1929, to what extent has it occurred elsewhere? While some may want to dismiss it as a perverse historical accident, Gastonia is far from unique when seen in the perspective of previous European and American experience. The tie between the church and the dominant classes of society has been a historical regularity and not a freak.

> 毫无疑问，Pope 的研究中最引人注目的发现，在于传教士对纺织工人的背弃程度之深。即便在意识形态层面未必如此，教会在经济层面与工厂管理层有着密不可分的联系。有组织的宗教是塑造易于操控的劳动力、以及抵制工会打破剥削现状之努力的关键工具。牧师们不仅为管理行为辩护；面对社区对工会组织者施加的暴力报复，他们更保持了沉默。但若 1929 年的 Gastonia 情况如此，这种现象在其他地方又达到了何种程度？尽管有人可能想将其视为反常的历史偶然，但从欧美过往经验的角度来看，Gastonia 绝非特例。教会与社会主导阶级之间的关联是一种历史常态，而非异常现象。

Recall first the Catholicism of medieval Europe. Perhaps more than any other religious form, medieval Catholicism is thought to have catered to all classes in its position as a monolithic institution. In fact, however, there is ample evidence that Catholicism paved the way for the Protestant Reformation by overidentifying with the secular elite. It was precisely in neglecting the lower and lower middle classes that it stimulated the demand for a new church with a more attentive doctrine and a more specialized appeal.

> 首先回顾中世纪 Europe 的天主教。或许比其他任何宗教形式都更甚，中世纪天主教被认为在其作为单一机构的位置上迎合了所有阶级。然而，事实上，有充分证据表明天主教通过过度认同世俗精英为 Protestant Reformation 铺平了道路。正是在忽视下层和中下层阶级时，它刺激了对一个拥有更专注教义和更专门化吸引力的新教会的需求。

G. G. Coulton offers some revealing examples. He indicates that the thirteenth-century Catholic affinity for the upper classes was so great that there was actually an attempt to reinterpret Jesus and his disciples as aristocratic gentlemen.[^0-1-6] Coulton cites a satirical catechism beseechung God to grant that the higher bourgeoisie might "make free with [the peasantry's] wives and daughters, and to rejoice in their death."[^0-1-7] He also notes an aphorism of the day which received the smiling assent of the clergy: "Three things are merciless when they get the upper hand--flood, fire, and the common folk."[^0-1-8] Nor is Coulton alone in perceiving the alliance between the church and the upper classes. Troeltsch, Burckhardt, Huizuinga, and Pirenne offer similar evidence.[^0-1-9] As a last instance, Pirenne departs from the conventional interpretation of the Gothic cathedral spires as soaring expressions of religious sensibility. He suggests that they were more realistically intended as village advertisements and beacons for commerce. It was in this spirit that the merchants donated their money and their enthusiasm; it was apparently for other reasons altogether that the peasantry donated their backs.

> G. G. Coulton 提供了一些揭示性的例子。他指出，13 世纪天主教对上层阶级的亲和力如此之大，以至于实际上有人试图将耶稣和他的门徒重新解释为贵族绅士。[^0-1-6] Coulton 引用了一个讽刺性的教义问答，恳求上帝允许上层资产阶级“随意对待 [农民] 的妻子和女儿，并为他们的死亡而欢欣。”[^0-1-7] 他还注意到当时的一句格言，得到了神职人员的微笑赞同：“三件事一旦得势便无情——洪水、火灾和普通民众。”[^0-1-8] 并非只有 Coulton 察觉到教会与上层阶级之间的联盟。Troeltsch、Burckhardt、Huizuinga 和 Pirenne 提供了类似的证据。[^0-1-9] 作为最后一个例子，Pirenne 背离了对哥特式大教堂尖塔的传统解释，即将其视为宗教情感的升华表达。他提出，它们更现实地旨在作为村庄的广告和商业的灯塔。正是本着这种精神，商人们捐赠了他们的金钱和热情；而农民们捐赠他们的劳力，显然完全是出于其他原因。

Moving on to the Reformation itself, Max Weber's analysis of The Protestant Ethic and the Spirit of Capitalism[^0-1-10] commands confrontation. It is true that Weber envisaged Protestantism as a crucial catalyst in a change of values and an important impetus to the rise of the bourgeoisie against the feudal nobility. At the same time, Weber was alert to a distinction between theology and the church as an institution. He cites German Lutheranism as an instance of the institution betraying the theology. He notes that many of the necessary refinements in the theology itself were at the demand of a disgruntled laity for whom complete predestination was an insufficient justification for the pursuit of economic success. Only a theology that posited success as a ticket to salvation was acceptable, and the pressure produced a gradual shift away from the thought of Calvin as well as Luther. Other scholars have added further support. R. H. Tawney, H. M. Robertson, and, most recently, Kurt Samuelson have accused Weber of not going far enough in noting the extent to which the policies of the church were determined by the laity.[^0-1-11] They argue that capitalism (even Weber's distinct species of "rational capitalism") existed before the Reformation. Insofar as Protestantism was any more sympathetic than Catholicism, it was precisely in order to attach itself to a rising class and a new type of societal dominance.

> 转向宗教改革本身，Max Weber 对《新教伦理与资本主义精神》[^0-1-10] 的分析值得深入探讨。诚然，Weber 将新教视为价值观变革的关键催化剂，也是资产阶级对抗封建贵族崛起的重要推动力。与此同时，Weber 敏锐地区分了神学与作为制度的教会。他以德国路德宗为例，指出制度背叛神学的现象。他注意到，神学本身许多必要的修正，正是出于平信徒阶层的不满——对他们而言，完全的预定论不足以解释追求经济成就的正当性。唯有将成功视为救赎凭证的神学才能被接受，这种压力导致思想逐渐偏离 Calvin 与 Luther 的原始主张。其他学者提供了进一步佐证。R. H. Tawney、H. M. Robertson 以及近期的 Kurt Samuelson 均指责 Weber 未能充分揭示教会政策受平信徒影响的程度[^0-1-11]。他们认为资本主义（甚至 Weber 所定义的独特“理性资本主义”）在宗教改革前已然存在。新教若比天主教更具亲和力，恰恰是为了依附于新兴阶级与社会主导形态。

Unhappily many of these critics have gone too far in denying Weber his due. While Protestantism may well have been more of a tool than a stimulant to the bourgeoisie, the Reformation was nevertheless important in shattering the dominance of Catholicism and in providing a climate in which traditionalism of all sorts suffered. Then too, it is possible to see a different sort of importance for Protestantism. Whether or not it provided a goad to the bourgeoisie, there is evidence that it was especially influential in providing a sop for the proletariat.

> 不幸的是，许多这些批评者走得太远，否认了 Weber 应得的赞誉。尽管新教可能更像是资产阶级的工具而非刺激，但新教改革在打破天主教的统治和提供一种各种传统主义都遭受打击的氛围方面仍然很重要。此外，也有可能看到新教改革的一种不同重要性。无论它是否刺激了资产阶级，有证据表明它在安抚无产阶级方面特别有影响力。

This point is made well by two recent studies of the rise of industry in eighteenth- and nineteenth-century England. Both Reinhard Bendix[^0-1-12] and Neil J. Smelser[^0-1-13] suggest that the influence of Methodism was greater among the workers than among their employers. Bendix, for example, cites the Society for Promoting Christian Knowledge, a kind of trade school run by the churches for the purpose of producing obedient servants who would serve their masters in the “Christian fashion.” This “fashion” followed Edmund Burke in his sanctification of the existing social structure as immutably dictated by “divine providence.” It is understandable, then, that many of the working class left the churches. K. S. Inglis points out as a postscript that, despite changes of heart and policy, British Protestantism was by and large unsuccessful in trying to woo back at the end of the nineteenth century the workers it had alienated at the beginning.[^0-1-14]

> 关于 18 至 19 世纪英国工业崛起的近期两项研究，很好地阐释了这一点。Reinhard Bendix[^0-1-12] 与 Neil J. Smelser[^0-1-13] 均指出，卫理公会派在工人群体中的影响力，要大于其对雇主阶层的影响。例如，Bendix 引证了基督教知识促进会的案例，该会是由教会运营的一类职业学校，旨在培养以“基督教方式”效忠主人的顺从仆人。此种“方式”追随 Edmund Burke 的思想，将现存社会结构神圣化为“神圣天命”所不可更改的旨意。因此，许多工人阶级选择离开教会，这便不难理解了。K. S. Inglis 补充指出，尽管心态与政策有所调整，但英国新教在 19 世纪末试图挽回其在世纪初疏远的工人群体方面，总体而言并未成功。

The situation was much the same in the United States. It is true that industrialization occurred later in this country, and that this offered the churches a chance to benefit from the lessons of their English predecessors. Yet the historian Henry F. May indicates that even so Protestantism was married to business and divorced from labor throughout the last century.[^0-1-15] In 1832, de Tocqueville commented with bitter irony that 

- *the religionists are the enemies of liberty and the friends of liberty attack religion; the high-minded and the noble advocate bondage, and the meanest and most servile preach independence; honest and enlightened citizens are opposed to all progress, whilst men without patriotism and without principle put themselves forward as the apostles of civilization and intelligence.[^0-1-16]*

> 美国的情况也大抵如此。诚然，该国的工业化进程起步较晚，这使教会得以从英国同行的经验中汲取教训。然而历史学家 Henry F. May 指出，即便如此，在整个上世纪，新教主义仍与商业紧密结合，却与劳工阶层渐行渐远。[^0-1-15] 1832 年，de Tocqueville 曾以尖锐的讽刺笔调评论道：
> 
> - 宗教人士成为自由的敌人，而自由的拥护者却在攻击宗教；高尚之士鼓吹奴役，最卑劣谄媚者却宣扬独立；正直开明的公民反对一切进步，而无爱国情操、无原则之人竟自诩为文明与智慧的使者。[^0-1-16]

Nor was de Tocqueville alone among early nineteenth-century foreign observers in deprecating the clergy. If de Tocqueville spoke from the perspective of a French Catholic elitist, Harriet Martineau spoke similarly as a British liberal Protestant:

- *The American clergy are the most backward and timid class in the society in which they live; self-exiled from the great moral questions of the time; the least informed with the true knowledge; the least efficient in virtuous action; the least conscious of that Christian and republican freedom which, as the native atmosphere of piety and holiness, it is their prime duty to cherish and diffuse.[^0-1-17]*

> 19 世纪初的外国观察者中，贬低神职人员的并非仅有 de Tocqueville 一人。如果说 de Tocqueville 是从法国天主教精英主义者的视角发言，那么 Harriet Martineau 则同样以英国自由派新教徒的身份表达了类似观点：
> 
> - 美国的神职人员是他们所处社会中最保守、最怯懦的阶层；他们自我放逐于时代的重大道德议题之外；对真知灼见最为匮乏；在践行美德方面最为低效；对于那种作为虔诚与圣洁天然氛围的基督教及共和主义自由，他们最缺乏意识，而弘扬与传播这种自由正是他们的首要职责。[^0-1-17]

Apparently there was little change in subsequent years. In 1878, the magazine of the Congregationalist Church had this to say about the migrant workers of the day:

- *They are profane, licentious, filthy, vermin-swarming thieves, petty robbers, and sometimes murderers, social pests and perambulatory nuisances; which require the immediate and stringent attention of the community. . . . We confess a strong feeling in favor toward the idea . . . that it might be well to revive for use in this connection the long obsolete whipping-post.[^0-1-18]*

> 显然，此后几年情况几乎没有变化。1878 年，公理会教会的杂志曾这样评论当时的移民工人：
> 
> - 他们是亵渎神明、放荡不羁、污秽不堪、蛆虫般滋生的窃贼、小偷，有时甚至是杀人犯，是社会的害虫和四处游荡的祸患；亟需社区立即采取严厉措施予以关注……我们坦承，我们对此观点怀有强烈的赞同之情……或许应当重新启用早已废弃的鞭刑柱，用于处理此类问题。[^0-1-18]

At the same time, Henry Ward Beecher, the prominent clergyman, was advising workers to rest content on a dollar a day for a family of six children since "water costs nothing; and a man who cannot live on bread is not fit to live." Meanwhile Beecher and his colleagues lived well indeed. One of these, Russell Conwell, delivered his famous "Acres of Diamonds" speech—a confection of laissez-faire, pro-management economics—some six thousand times for some eight million dollars, according to his own estimate.

> 与此同时，杰出的神职人员 Henry Ward Beecher 正建议工人们满足于每天一美元的收入来养活一个有六个孩子的家庭，因为“水是免费的；而一个仅靠面包无法生存的人不配活着。”然而 Beecher 和他的同僚们却生活得相当优渥。其中一位名为 Russell Conwell 的牧师，曾发表他著名的“Acres of Diamonds”演讲——这是一场融合了自由放任主义、亲管理阶层经济理念的精心之作——据他自己估计，这场演讲进行了约六千次，为他带来了约八百万美元的收入。

Much of this came to a head in the North in the last two decades of the century. After a series of depressions, the Pullman strike, the Haymarket affair and various similar incidents, labor began to attract more sympathy, and some of the churches began to reconsider their economic theory. The Social Gospel Movement was founded by Washington Gladden, a Congregationalist, by Frances Willard, the socialist founder of the W.C.T.U., and by others. The movement is generally considered a marked shift away from management and toward labor, away from conservatism and toward progressivism, away from laissez-faire and toward responsible economic planning. But, according to May, it was a disappointment. The Social Gospel did not actually espouse the cause of labor, though it did recognize labor's right to collective action. One of its fundamental premises was that labor strife was caused by misguided heathens who needed only Christian conversion to see the light of docility.

> 这种情况在北方于该世纪的最后二十年达到了高潮。经历了一系列的经济萧条、普尔曼大罢工、干草市场事件及各类类似事件后，劳工阶层开始获得更多同情，部分教会也开始重新审视其经济理论。社会福音运动由公理会教徒 Washington Gladden、妇女基督教戒酒联合会（W.C.T.U.）的社会主义创始人 Frances Willard 等人发起。该运动通常被视为一次显著转向：从资方转向劳方，从保守主义转向进步主义，从自由放任转向负责任的经济规划。但根据 May 的观点，这一运动令人失望。社会福音运动并未真正支持劳工事业，尽管它承认劳工集体行动的权利。其基本前提之一是：劳资冲突是由误入歧途的非信徒引起的，这些人只需皈依基督教便能领悟顺从之道。

Clearly, then, Gastonia in the 1920's was hardly an anomaly in the perspective of the past. The church, like any institution, has depended upon the favor of those in power, and it has often gained that favor by justifying the actions of the elite and tempering the reactions of the "masses." But while it may be too much to assert with Weber that Protestantism provided an indispensable condition for the revolution of capitalism, it is also excessive to rely on Marx's dictum that religion is the "opiate of the masses." The church is both more active and more dynamic than Marx's metaphor would have it. Indeed, there is a very real sense in which the last 35 years have produced a sweeping change in the church's posture toward the economy in particular and the community as a whole. Nowhere is this more clearly suggested than in the changing context of the American community.

> 显然，那么，从历史的角度审视，Gastonia 在 1920 年代几乎算不上一个特例。教会如同任何机构一样，始终依赖于当权者的青睐，且常常通过为精英行为辩护并缓和“群众”反应来换取这种青睐。然而，尽管随 Weber 断言 Protestantism 为 capitalism 革命提供了不可或缺的条件或许言过其实，但仅凭 Marx 所谓宗教即“群众鸦片”的定论也同样有失偏颇。教会远比 Marx 的隐喻所描述的更为积极与能动。事实上，在过去的 35 年间，教会在经济层面乃至整体社区姿态上确实发生了翻天覆地的变化。这一点在美国社区变迁的语境中体现得最为清晰。

---

## Structural Differentiation and the Contemporary American Community
**结构分化与当代美国社区**

Millhands and Preachers was part of a wave of community studies that preoccupied sociologists in the 1930's. Subsequent studies have added to the tradition so that by now the literature of research on the American community is much richer than it was when Pope began his analysis. Some of this literature addresses problems very similar to Pope's. Other parts of it have valuable secondary insights and say a good deal by implication. Even a partial list of the relevant works would include Robert and Helen Lynd's two volumes on Middletown, or Muncie, Indiana; Lloyd Warner's Yankee City series on Newburyport, Massachusetts; Floyd Hunter's study of Community Power Structure in Atlanta, Georgia; Robert Dahl's analysis of Who Governs? in New Haven, Connecticut; Kenneth Underwood's exploration of Protestant and Catholic tensions in Holyoke, Massachusetts; John Morland's depiction of the Millways of Kent, a town very much like Gastonia; and the analysis by Arthur Vidich and Joseph Bensman of a Small Town in Mass Society in upper New York State. [^0-1-19]

> 《Millhands and Preachers》是 20 世纪 30 年代社会学家聚焦的社区研究浪潮中的一部分。随后的研究延续了这一传统，使得如今关于美国社区的文献资料远比 Pope 开始其分析时更为丰富。其中部分文献探讨的问题与 Pope 的研究极为相似。其他部分则提供了有价值的次要见解，并蕴含丰富的引申意义。即使仅列举部分相关著作，也应包括 Robert 与 Helen Lynd 关于印第安纳州曼西镇的两卷本研究、Lloyd Warner 关于马萨诸塞州纽伯里波特的《Yankee City》系列、Floyd Hunter 对佐治亚州亚特兰大《Community Power Structure in Atlanta》的研究、Robert Dahl 对康涅狄格州纽黑文市《Who Governs?》的分析、Kenneth Underwood 对马萨诸塞州霍利奥克市新教与天主教紧张关系的探索、John Morland 对 Kent 郡（一个与加斯托尼亚极为相似的城镇）纺织业社区的描绘，以及 Arthur Vidich 与 Joseph Bensman 对纽约州北部《Small Town in Mass Society》的分析。[^0-1-19]

Taken together these studies document the changing nature of American communities. As the title of Maurice Stein's recent book suggests, they point to a deepening Eclipse of Community.[^0-1-20] Stein's point is that the processes of industrialization, urbanization, and bureaucratization are destroying the self-contained community and subverting its traditional gemütlichkeit. Seen from a somewhat different perspective, these studies show an increasing "structural differentiation."[^0-1-21] In this process, institutions are pulled out of the close articulation that characterizes the undifferentiated community. Politics, education, the family, the economy, and even religion become more specialized and more autonomous. The possibility of one dominating another grows more remote as each becomes an island unto itself. Each institution is likely to have more contact with its national affiliates than with different institutions in the same community. The community is apt to lose some of its local self-determination as its parts become subject to bureaucratic decisions at the national rather than the community level. Labor disputes, church policy, political platforms, and educational programs are all increasingly settled “at the top.” The community must adapt rather than initiate.

> 综合这些研究，我们可以看出美国社区性质的变化。正如 Maurice Stein 近期著作标题所揭示的，这些研究共同指向了日益加深的《Eclipse of Community》[^0-1-20]。Stein 的核心观点是，工业化、城市化和官僚化的进程正在摧毁自给自足的社区，并侵蚀其传统的温馨氛围。从稍有不同的视角来看，这些研究显示了一种日益增强的“结构分化”[^0-1-21]。在这个过程中，各种制度从紧密的联结中被剥离出来，而这种紧密联结正是未分化社区的特征。政治、教育、家庭、经济乃至宗教都变得更加专业化和自主化。随着每个领域都成为自成一体的孤岛，一个领域主导另一个领域的可能性变得越来越渺茫。同一社区内的不同机构之间，其联系很可能弱于它们各自与全国性分支机构之间的联系。随着社区的各个组成部分日益受到国家层面而非社区层面的官僚决策制约，社区可能会丧失一部分地方自治权。劳资纠纷、教会政策、政治纲领以及教育方案，都越来越多地由“高层”决定。社区必须适应，而非主动开创。

If structural differentiation is the trend of the present, Pope's Gastonia may be a scene from the past. There, crucial community cleavages were vertical (between high and low status groups) instead of horizontal (between the distinct provinces of autonomous institutions). The mills and the churches were necessarily intertwined. Lacking the middle ground of neutrality, the churches had to choose between supporting or opposing mill management, and the latter course led to organizational collapse. This absence of differentiation is reflected in the currents of "localism." Whereas the cosmopolitan, differentiated community is apt to look to national levels for leadership, the local community is apt to view national leadership with suspicion and even hostility. Whereas the cosmopolitan, differentiated institution is likely to find primary succor from its national hierarchy, the local, undifferentiated institution is more apt to make its peace with institutions of other stripes in the same community. There is ample evidence of the dominant localism in Gastonia. Both the inception and the resolution of the Loray strike are cases in point.

> 如果结构分化是当下的趋势，那么 Pope 笔下的 Gastonia 或许呈现了一幅过去的景象。在那里，关键的社区分裂是垂直的（存在于高地位与低地位群体之间），而非水平的（存在于自治机构的不同领域之间）。工厂与教会必然相互交织。由于缺乏中立地带，教会必须在支持或反对工厂管理层之间做出选择，而选择后者往往导致组织崩溃。这种分化的缺失反映在“地方主义”的思潮中。世界主义的、分化的社区倾向于寻求国家层面的领导，而地方社区则倾向于以怀疑甚至敌视的态度看待国家领导。世界主义的、分化的机构更可能从其国家层级获得主要支持，而地方的、未分化的机构则更倾向于与同一社区内其他类型的机构达成和解。有充分证据表明 Gastonia 存在主导性的地方主义。Loray 罢工的发起与解决都是鲜明的例证。

Millhands and Preachers is not as clear as it might be on the conditions prompting the strike. But if the strike had been launched solely around the issues of better wages and working conditions, there is every reason to believe that it would not have gone as far as it did. Instead, one of its major grievances was the northern ownership that had bought out many of the original southern entrepreneurs. Not only did these "outside" owners seek to instill outside standards of efficiency by means of the "stretch-out" (in which the worker is asked to tend more machines for the same wage), but the new owners also began to do away with "paternalism," the keystone of southern textile labor relations, in which management provided housing, schooling, and seeming sympathy to the worker. It is significant that most of the strikes during the era covered by the book occurred in absentee-owned mills. It is equally noteworthy that the wave of strikes ebbed after 1929, when management reestablished many of the old paternalistic customs in an effort to produce a simulated localism that would assuage the bitterness. Pope, for example, mentions the later use of mill village ministers to check on the "reliability" of job recruits and to inform the managers of worker discontent. Such a link between management and the churches was a key aspect of localism itself.

> 《Millhands and Preachers》 对引发罢工的具体条件描述得并不十分清晰。但若罢工仅围绕提高工资和改善工作条件这两个问题展开，那么完全有理由相信，罢工不会发展到如此深远的程度。相反，其主要不满之一是被北方所有权收购了许多原始南方企业家。这些“外部”所有者不仅试图通过“拉伸”（即要求工人在相同工资下照看更多机器）来灌输外部效率标准，而且新所有者还开始废除“家长式管理”，这是南方纺织劳工关系的基石，其中管理层提供住房、教育和表面上的同情给工人。值得注意的是，书中涵盖的时代大多数罢工发生在由外地所有者拥有的工厂中。同样值得注意的是，罢工浪潮在 1929 年后消退，当时管理层重新建立了许多旧的家长式习俗，以努力制造一种模拟的地方主义来缓解痛苦。例如，Pope 提到后来使用工厂村庄的牧师来检查求职者的“可靠性”，并向经理报告工人的不满。这种管理层与教会之间的联系是地方主义本身的一个关键方面。

Although the book does not point up the influence of outside management in precipitating the strike, it is richly detailed in portraying the reaction to outside union organizers as crucial to the strike's demise. Initially the strike was looked upon with some sympathy in the community. As the days wore on, favor turned to hostility when mill management labeled the strike leaders "foreign agitators" and received the help of the police, the clergy, and the local press in making the label stick. It seems that neither outside owners nor outside unionists were welcome in Gastonia. It is possible that a more indigenous union might have carried the day, as it did five years later in the shoe industry in Newburyport. There the union was able to galvanize local interests in a battle against the exploitation of absentee-owners in New York.[^0-1-22] But both Gastonia and the Newburyport of the 1930's may be contrasted with the situation of countless towns today having branches of, say, the automobile industry. Here, labor-management disputes are settled en masse in Detroit. The results are then communicated down the line to a visiting and passive community that avoids the violence but is also largely gerrymandered out of the decision-making process.[^0-1-23]

> 尽管本书并未强调外部管理在引发罢工中的作用，但是却以丰富细节描绘了社区对外部工会组织者的反应如何成为罢工失败的关键。起初，社区对罢工抱有一定同情。随着时间推移，当工厂管理层将罢工领袖贴上“外来煽动者”标签，并借助警方、神职人员和地方媒体使这一标签深入人心时，公众态度便由支持转为敌意。显然，无论是外部资方还是外部工会组织者，在 Gastonia 都不受欢迎。若是一个更具本土根基的工会组织，或许能赢得胜利，正如五年后 Newburyport 制鞋业发生的那样——该地工会成功凝聚了地方利益，以对抗纽约外部工厂业主的剥削。但 Gastonia 与 1930 年代的 Newburyport 情形，均可与当今无数拥有汽车工业分支工厂的城镇现状形成对比。在这些地方，劳资纠纷通常在 Detroit 被集中解决。决议结果随后层层下达至那些被动接收的访察社区，这些社区虽避免了暴力冲突，却也大多被排除在决策进程之外。

What are the implications of structural differentiation for religion? We have already mentioned that in nondifferentiated communities the church is frequently forced to take sides whenever conflict occurs. Moreover, it is generally necessary for it to side with the dominant party whether this is the feudal nobility, the rising bourgeoisie, the industrial entrepreneurs at the end of the nineteenth century, or the Gastonia mill management. But differentiation conduces to a new neutrality. In an age of specialization, the church is often ignorant of the intricacies of conflict in other areas. In an age of bureaucratization, this conflict is generally resolved at the highest reaches of bureaucracies that are impenetrable to church influence.

> 结构分化对宗教意味着什么？我们已提及，在未分化的社群中，每当冲突发生时，教会往往被迫选边站队。此外，无论主导方是封建贵族、新兴资产阶级、19 世纪末的工业企业家，还是 Gastonia 工厂管理层，教会通常都必须站在主导方一边。但分化促成了新的中立性。在专业化的时代，教会常对其他领域冲突的复杂性一无所知。在官僚化的时代，这类冲突通常在官僚体系高层得以解决，而教会的影响力难以渗透其中。

For all these reasons, the church is often put in the position of commentator rather than combatant. Once relegated to the periphery, it both gains and loses. We are not asserting that the church is better off in either the differentiated or the nondifferentiated community. Is it preferable to be the captive of the dominant forces or to be defined as irrelevant? Is it better to pay the price of vassalage for the prize of community involvement or to pay the price of irrelevance for the prize of ideological freedom? The point is not that there is no longer a dilemma but rather that the nature of the dilemma has changed. This is, of course, an oversimplification, and later we will comment on several other factors that influence the church's position in secular affairs. But, in the meantime, let us examine some of the evidence for the effects of differentiation itself.

> 正因如此，教会往往被置于评论者而非战斗者的位置。一旦被边缘化，它既有所得，也有所失。我们并非断言教会在分化或未分化的社群中必然处于更优状态。究竟是成为主导势力的附庸更可取，还是被定义为无关紧要者更合适？是为换取社群参与的资格付出附庸的代价更好，还是为获得意识形态自由付出被边缘化的代价更佳？问题的关键不在于困境已不复存在，而在于困境的本质已然改变。当然，这是一种过度简化的表述，后续我们将探讨影响教会在世俗事务中定位的其他若干因素。但此刻，让我们先审视关于分化本身所产生影响的一些证据。

Virtually all the community studies offer support. Underwood's research in Holyoke finds that even the local Catholic priest with a working-class parish does not accede to the union's request for backing. Union affairs have simply grown much too complex, and he prefers to ignore them altogether. Hunter points out that, although Atlanta ministers are frequently important for executing a policy once it is determined, they have very little influence in determining what that policy will be.

> 几乎所有社区研究都提供了支持。Underwood 在 Holyoke 的研究发现，即使是服务于工人阶级教区的当地天主教神父，也并未应允工会的支持请求。工会事务已变得过于复杂，他更倾向于完全不予理会。Hunter 指出，尽管亚特兰大的牧师们常在政策确定后的执行阶段发挥重要作用，但他们对于政策本身的制定几乎毫无影响力。

Dahl rarely mentions the churches or the clergy in his study of New Haven. He does so only to contrast the current situation with the Congregationalist theocracy of the nineteenth century and to note that, contrary to several allegations, the Catholics have exerted surprisingly little pressure on the administration of the public schools. Lloyd Warner continually suggests the unimportance of religion for the administration of the shoe factories. Although Newburyport is known as a "weak union town," he, in contrast to Pope, conspicuously avoids citing religion as one of the factors in making it so.

> Dahl 在其对 New Haven 的研究中很少提及教会或神职人员。他这样做仅是为了将现状与十九世纪的公理会神权政治进行对比，并指出，与一些指控相反，天主教徒对公立学校的管理施加了令人惊讶的微小压力。Lloyd Warner 不断暗示宗教对鞋厂管理的重要性微乎其微。尽管纽伯里波特被称为“工会薄弱之城”，但与 Pope 不同，他明显避免将宗教列为造成此状况的因素之一。

By all odds the most persuasive evidence of this different plight of the churches comes from the Lynds' research in Muncie, Indiana. The Lynds and Pope were concerned with the same time period, but Muncie was even then far larger and more differentiated than Gastonia. The dominant theme of the Lynds' study is that of "secularization"—the decline of traditional values and an increasing willingness to subject any value to dispassionate criticism and innovation. Since religion crystallizes much of tradition, it is especially vulnerable. Not only had there been a de-emphasis of religious doctrine but there had also been a tendency to reserve the churches exclusively for Sundays. The local business leaders seemed to shy away from the clergy wherever possible. Ministers were not invited into the Rotary Club. While there were some instances of supplemental salary "gifts," these seemed to be intended more to salve the conscience for an impeccable clergy than to buy their influence. As one woman reacted to a minister who had a bit of inherited wealth, "it was so nice to have a minister's wife one did not pity." In the Lynds' own words, the ministers can be found "eagerly lingering about the fringes of things trying to get a chance to talk to the men of the city, who in turn are diffident about talking frankly to them."[^0-1-24]

> 毫无疑问，最能证明教会这种不同处境的有力证据，来自 Lynd 夫妇在印第安纳州 Muncie 的研究。Lynd 夫妇与 Pope 关注的是同一时期，但即便在当时，Muncie 的规模也远大于 Gastonia，且社会结构更为分化。Lynd 夫妇研究的核心主题是“世俗化”——即传统价值观的衰落，以及人们越来越倾向于对任何价值观进行冷静批判与革新。由于宗教凝结了大量传统，它尤其容易受到冲击。不仅宗教教义被淡化，还出现了将教会活动仅仅局限于星期天的趋势。当地商业领袖似乎尽可能回避与神职人员接触。牧师并未被邀请加入 Rotary Club。尽管存在一些补充薪水的“赠礼”情况，但这些似乎更多是为了安抚良心——以维持神职人员无可指摘的形象，而非收买其影响力。正如一位女性对一位拥有少许继承财富的牧师所作出的反应：“有一位无需让人同情的牧师妻子，真是太好了。”用林德夫妇自己的话说，牧师们常常“急切地徘徊在各类事务的边缘，试图寻找机会与城市中的男性交谈，而这些男性却往往不愿对他们坦诚相待。”[^0-1-24]

It is possible that much of the difference between Muncie and Gastonia concerns the lack of crisis in the former. The Lynds were aware of the analytic one-sidedness of focusing solely on stability and prosperity. Hence they returned to Muncie in the midst of the depression in 1934, some 10 years after their original research. While they themselves hypothesized that the churches would become more meaningful in a time of crisis, they found no evidence of this. As one leading minister put it: "In the old days people went to preachers for consolation, information, and inspiration. They still come to us for consolation, but go to the newspapers for information and inspiration."[^0-1-25] Here is a clear example of differentiation; and since much of the consoling function rested on other-worldly premises, it fits well with the Lynds' over-all conclusions:

- Middletown's churches appear to be forever bartering the opportunity for leadership in the area of change for the right to continue a shadowy leadership in the Changeless, as the church defines the latter.[^0-1-26]

> Muncie 与 Gastonia 之间的差异很大程度上可能源于前者未经历危机。Lynd 夫妇意识到仅关注稳定与繁荣在分析上存在片面性，因此他们于 1934 年经济大萧条期间重返 Muncie，这距离他们最初的研究已过去约十年。尽管他们曾假设教会在危机时期会变得更具意义，但并未找到相关证据。正如一位主要牧师所言：“过去人们向传教士寻求慰藉、信息与灵感；如今他们仍向我们寻求慰藉，却转向报纸获取信息与灵感。”[^0-1-25] 这清晰地展现了功能分化的实例；由于慰藉功能很大程度上依托于超世俗的前提，该现象与 Lynd 夫妇的整体结论高度吻合。
> 
> - Middletown 的各个教会，似乎永远在用引领变革的机会，去换取在非变革领域中继续维持一种模糊领导权的权利——正如教会对后者的界定那样。[^0-1-26]

But the concept of structural differentiation provides an even broader sweep than the distinction between Muncie and Gastonia. Though the intervening history is grossly oversimplified, Pope's Gastonia is analogous to pretwentiemth century Europe in its lack of differentiation. Conversely the Lynds' Muncie is a better representative of twentieth-century Western society precisely because of its differentiation. Weber himself was aware of the distinction. In some often neglected passages at the end of The Protestant Ethic and the Spirit of Capitalism, he predicted that fully developed capitalism would no longer need the support of ascetic Protestantism.[^0-1-27] Once on its feet, capitalism would proceed relatively independently, engendering its own values and compelling submission with its own authority.

> 但结构分化的概念所涵盖的范围，远比 Muncie 与 Gastonia 之间的区别更为广阔。尽管其中涉及的历史被极度简化，Pope 所描述的 Gastonia 因其缺乏分化，可与 20 世纪前的欧洲相类比。相反，Lynd 夫妇笔下的 Muncie 正是由于其分化特征，更能代表 20 世纪的西方社会。Weber 本人也意识到了这一区别。在《The Protestant Ethic and the Spirit of Capitalism》结尾处一些常被忽略的段落中，他预言完全成熟的资本主义将不再需要禁欲新教的支持。[^0-1-27] 一旦站稳脚跟，资本主义将相对独立地发展，衍生出其自身的价值观，并以自身的权威迫使人们服从。

---

Morland, Millways of Kent (Chapel Hill, University of North Carolina Press, 1958); Arthur J. Perhaps the most influential analysis has been Ferdinand Tonnie's *Gemeinschaft und Gesellschaft* written in 1887 and available in English as *Community and Society* (New York, Harper, 1963). More recent scholars have portrayed the demise of community within the framework of the "mass society." See, for example, David Riesman, *The Lonely Crowd* (New Haven, Yale University Press, 1950); William Kornhauser, *The Politics of Mass Society* (Glencoe, The Free Press, 1959); Robert A. For their treatment in the anthropological literature, see the discussion of the research of Robert Redfield and Oscar Lewis on *Tepoztlan*, Mexico, in Horace Miner, "The Folk-Urban Continuum," in Paul F. The former is well demonstrated by Robert Havighurst and H. Gerthon Morgan, *The Social History of a War Boom Community* (New York, Longmans, Green, 1951); and Lowell J. Carr and James E. Stermer, Willow Run: A Study in Industrialization and Cultural Inadequacy (New York, Harper, 1952). Two trenchant analyses of relocation are Charles R. Walker, Steeltown (New York, Harper, 1950) and W. F. Cottwell, "Death by Dieselization: A Case Study in the Reaction to Technological Change," American Sociological Review, 16 (June, 1951), 358-365.
